Specific Actions

              INITIATIVE 3.5: CUSTOMER EXPANSION PROGRAM                          

                                                                                  
  EXPANSION OPPORTUNITY ANALYSIS                                                  
    
                                                                                  
  Current Service Mix:                                                            
   Deferred Cash Plan Admin: 69% of revenue                                  
   Carry/Coinvestment Admin: 30% of revenue                                  
   Share Plan Admin: 1% of revenue                                           
                                                                                  
  Expansion Opportunities:                                                        
   Cross-sell: Customers using 1 service  2-3 services                      
   Upsell: Expand scope within current service                               
   Price optimization: Value-based pricing alignment                         
                                                                                  
  WORKSTREAM A: CUSTOMER SEGMENTATION & ANALYSIS                                 
    
  Owner: Client Success Lead with Sales                                          
  Timeline: Month 8-9                                                            
                                                                                  
  Actions:                                                                       
   Analyze all customers by:                                                 
      Current services used                                                 
      Contract value and tenure                                             
      Growth potential (company growth, hiring)                             
      Whitespace (services they could use)                                  
                                                                                
   Score expansion potential:                                                
      High: Clear whitespace + strong relationship                          
      Medium: Potential opportunity + good relationship                     
      Low: Fully penetrated or relationship challenges                      
                                                                                
   Prioritize top 25 expansion accounts                                      
                                                                                  
  WORKSTREAM B: QUARTERLY BUSINESS REVIEW (QBR) PROGRAM                          
    
  Owner: Client Success Lead                                                     
  Timeline: Month 9-12

Governance Structure

                    TRANSFORMATION GOVERNANCE STRUCTURE                           

                                                                                  
  STEERING COMMITTEE                                                              
    
  Composition: CEO, CFO, COO, VP People, 2 Advisory Board Members               
  Cadence: Monthly                                                               
  Role: Strategic oversight, major decision approval, resource allocation       
                                                                                  
  TRANSFORMATION MANAGEMENT OFFICE (TMO)                                         
    
  Lead: COO or designated transformation lead                                    
  Cadence: Weekly                                                                
  Role: Cross-initiative coordination, risk management, reporting               
                                                                                  
  INITIATIVE OWNERS                                                               
    
  Assigned per initiative (as documented)                                        
  Cadence: Weekly status updates to TMO                                         
  Role: Day-to-day execution, milestone delivery, issue escalation              
                                                                                  
  REPORTING CADENCE                                                               
    
  Weekly:   Initiative dashboards to TMO                                        
  Monthly:  Steering committee executive summary                                
  Quarterly: Board/advisory comprehensive review                                
                                                                                  
  DECISION AUTHORITY                                                              
    
  <$25K budget change:     Initiative Owner                                     
  $25K-$100K budget change: TMO Lead                                            
  >$100K budget change:    Steering Committee                                   
  Timeline change >2 weeks: Steering Committee                                  
  Scope change (major):    Steering Committee

Conclusion

The Transformation Imperative

EWM Global possesses exceptional foundational assets98% customer retention, $1M lifetime values, and robust technology infrastructurethat represent significant strategic value. However, these assets are constrained by critical gaps in financial resilience, leadership capacity, and organizational culture that limit growth potential and create risk.

This 18-month implementation roadmap provides a sequenced, actionable path to transform EWM Global from a company with unrealized potential into a high-performing, scalable organization positioned for sustainable 20%+ growth and strategic optionality.

Key Transformation Principles

  1. Sequence matters: Address critical constraints (cash, leadership) before pursuing growth initiatives
  2. Quick wins build momentum: Early success creates organizational confidence for larger changes
  3. People first: Culture and leadership investments enable all other improvements
  4. Measure relentlessly: Track KPIs weekly, adjust monthly, report quarterly
  5. Protect customer excellence: Never compromise the 98% retention during transformation

Call to Action

The roadmap is clear. The investment case is compelling ($3M investment for $54-106M value creation). The risk of inactioncontinued constraint, competitive erosion, and value destructionis significant.

The time to begin is now.

Immediate Next Steps (Next 30 Days)

  1. CEO/Board Alignment: Review and approve transformation roadmap and investment
  2. Advisory Board Charter: Finalize and begin candidate outreach
  3. VP People Search: Engage executive search firm
  4. Financial Stabilization: Launch AR acceleration and credit facility discussions
  5. Weekly Leadership Cadence: Implement immediately
  6. Communication: Announce transformation commitment to organization

This implementation roadmap was developed based on comprehensive analysis across ten strategic dimensions. Execution should be adapted based on emerging learnings and changing circumstances, with regular review and adjustment through the governance structure outlined above.
